X Y is the scientific theory that Earth's lithosphere is divided into several large, rigid Xs that glide slowly over a hotter, plastic-like mantle layer called asthenosphere. [2026-02-22T17:47:57Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 4.	The available scientific evidence for plate tectonics doesn’t rely on just the current shapes of the continents or undersea plate boundaries that we can see. Wegener himself recognized a different kind of evidence when archaeologists working in two different countries X and Y independently found fossils of Mesosaurus, a 300 million-year old extinct reptile species. From the bones, paleontologists deduced that it was a freshwater species that thrived in shallow streams and rivers. The only problem is that over 4,000 km of saltwater ocean separates X and Y now, and there is no way the freshwater species would have been able to migrate that distance. Wegener argued that this is conclusive evidence the animal had simple walked across land between X and Y when they were joined together in a supercontinent. ID X and Y. ‎image omitted

Before Pangea existed (over 300 million years ago), and again after it split apart (around 200 million years ago), the Earth's southern landmasses (South America, Africa, Antarctica, Australia, and India) were joined together. In the late 1800s, an Austrian geologist named Eduard Suess realized these continents used to be connected because he found identical fossilized fern leaves on all of them. Because some of the most crucial rock and fossil evidence was found in a region of central India inhabited by the indigenous X people — and because the Sanskrit word Y means "forest" — he combined these two words to name the giant landmass Z. [2026-02-23T07:48:36Z] Pranshu: Within the core of a single strand of ultra-pure glass, microscopic density fluctuations are "frozen" during the manufacturing process. When a laser pulse is sent through, these imperfections cause a tiny fraction of the light to bounce back to the source—a phenomenon known as Rayleigh scattering. ↵ In modern geophysics, by monitoring the changes in optical phase of these returning echoes through X one can record earthquakes, volcanic tremors, as it (referring to X) microscopically stretches or compresses effectively turning it into a virtual seismometers. ↵ Identify X which is commonly used in a different industry for a completely different purpose.

[2026-02-23T17:35:46Z] Smit D Mahajani: This is the entirety of the part about Korea from the full letter: ↵ "My dear Jawaharlal, ↵ Thank you for your letters dated 29 and 30 June 1950 respectively. ↵ I have seen the statement on Korea. While it is satisfactory in its support of the UNO’s recommendation, I feel that we need not have reiterated our foreign policy. Such reiteration implies that this step could be construed as a departure from that policy and we were being apologetic or on the defensive about it. After all, the step which we have taken fits in with our policy of supporting the UNO and invoking the various remedies mentioned in the Charter against aggression. Once we felt, as we did in the case of Korea, that an aggression had taken place, I do not think we can set any limits to our action to resist that aggression. We have to exhaust all the means laid down in the Charter. The question merely would be one of timing and effectiveness. When actual armed aggression takes place, it is doubtful whether negotiations and mediation alone can secure the objective of peace. Negotiations and mediation can avail us only if there is a cessation of hostilities. Otherwise we cannot match words against arms."
